**Beer**

**Discover Morrisons' extensive range of quality beers. Our beer aisle is packed with some brilliant brews, including craft beers(opens in a new window), bitters and everything in between. Whether you're stocking up for your weekly shop or planning a special event, our beer essentials have got you covered. From casual get-togethers to proper celebrations, we've got the perfect pint. Choose from rich, full-bodied bitters(opens in a new window) or refreshing craft beers for your evening relaxation, all part of our high-quality beer range.**
